\bentry
\wordRemoveSpace{N,-n}{N, n}
\pron{enf}
\gl{\nA}
\expl{(\bava\ \eng{Ns} yA \eng{N's}).}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} iMgilxSf vaNaRmAleya hadinAlakxneya akaSxra. 
\num{2} mudarxNadalilx agalada mAna (= \hyperref{kandict_e.pdf}{E}{en}{en}.) 
\num{3} (\biVga) enf: \eng{N;} anidiRSaTx sithxra saMKeyx. 
\num{4} (\Bwvi) avogADorx sithxra(da saMkeVta). 
\enum
\emng

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}
\expl{}
\bmng
\eng{to the nth} (\engit{or} \eng{nth) degree} 
\banum
\alnum{a} yAvudAdarU beVkAda GAtakekx. 
\alnum{b} (\rUpa) eSaTxkekx beVkAdarU; paramAvadhige. 
\eanum
\emng
\eentry

\bentry

\pron{neVlf}
\gl{\nA}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} uguru; naKa. 
\num{2} (maqgagaLa, hakikxgaLa kAlina) moneyuguru. 
\num{3} (maqdu kokikxna hakikxgaLa) kokikxna meVlABxgadalilxna uguru padAthaRda gaTiTxgaMti. 
\num{4} moLe; ANi. 
\num{5} gajada \eng{1/16} BAga; \eng{$2\frac\bg 1\eg \bg 4\eg$} aMgula (hiMde baLasutitxdadx baTeTxya oMdu aLate). 
\enum
\emng

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} \eng{bite one's nail} (aBAyxsabaladiMda yA tALemxgeTuTx) uguru kaDi. 
\num{2} \eng{drive nail in one's} \hyperref{kandict_c.pdf}{C}{coffin(1)nuga}{$^1$coffin}. 
\numi{3} \eng{hard as nails} 
\banum
\alnum{a} daqDhakAyanAgi; gaTiTxmuTATxgi. 
\alnum{b} kalelxdeya; nidaRya; kaThiNa. 
\hypertarget{nailpagu4}{} 
\eanum
\numie
\numi{4} \eng{hit the nail on the head} 
\banum
\alnum{a} sariyAda sapxSaTxne koDu. 
\alnum{b} yAvudu sariyoV A kelasa mADu. 
\alnum{c} gurimuTuTx. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{5} \eng{hit the right nail}= \hyperlink{nailpagu4}{?pagu?\((4)\)}. 
\num{6} \eng{nail -- biting} tiVvarx AtaMkavanunxMTumADuva. 
\num{7} \eng{on the nail} (\kanmu\ haNa pAvatiya \vi) takaSxNa; kUDaleV; taDavilalxde. 
\num{8} \eng{right as nails} sari; nija; Kare; KaMDita sari. 
\num{9} \eng{tooth and nail} shakitxyanenxlAlx biTuTx; balavAgi paTuTx hiDidu: \eng{fight tooth and nail} balavAgi paTuTx hiDidu hoVrADu. 
\enum
\emng

\bentry
\word{naked}
\pron{neVkiDf}
\gl{\gu}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} naganx; betatxleya; nivARNa; baTeTx toTiTxrada; barimeYyina; nivaRsanada: \eng{as naked as my mother bore me} namamxmamx haDedAga heVgidedxnoV aMtha batatxle sithxtiyalilx. 
\num{2} arakiSxta; sulaBavAgi guriyAda, sikikxda; rakaSxNe ilalxda: \eng{left naked to temptations} sulaBavAgi parxloVBanegaLige sikikxda. 
\num{3} oreyilalxda; kApilalxda: \eng{a naked sword} oreyiMdeLeda katitx. 
\num{4} naganx; mucucxmareyilalxda; sapxSaTx; suPxTa; neVravAda: \eng{naked truth} naganxsatayx. 
\num{5} (pariVkeSxgAgi hodike) terediTaTx: \eng{his naked soul} avana terediTaTx Atamx. 
\num{6} baTaTxbayalAda; maragiDagaLilalxda; baMjaru: \eng{naked shores} baTaTx bayalAda karAvaLi. 
\num{7} rahita; ilalxda. 
\num{8} elegaLilalxda; boVLAda: \eng{naked trees} boVLu maragaLu.

\num{10} (nelada \vi) maNuNx, giDagaMTegaLiMda mucicxrada.

\alnum{a} tUkaDisutitxruvAga hiDi; nidedx hoVgutitxruvAga hiDi. 
\alnum{b} (ecacxrikeyiMda ilalxdiruvAga yA suLivukoDade) haThAtAtxgi hiDiduhAku. 
\alnum{c} (kataRvayxvanunx alakiSxsutitxruvAga yA adaralilx tapupx mADutitxruvAga) Pakakxne hiDi; aniriVkiSxtavAgi hiDidu hAku. 
\eanum
\emng
\eentry

\bnum

\num{2} parxkaqtisidadhx. 
\numi{3} (\saM) sahaja; sAvxBAvika: 
\banum
\alnum{a} (savxrada \vi) tAravAgali maMdarxvAgali Agirada. 
\alnum{b} (rAgaparxsAtxrada \vi) tAra savxragaLAgali maMdarx savxragaLAgali ilalxdiruva. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{4} rUDhiya; sAvxBAvikavAda; sAmAnayx vayxvahArada. 
\num{5} pArxkaqtika; neYsagiRka; sAvxBAvika; nAgarikateya parxBAvavilalxda yA dhamaR saMsAkxra \mo vugaLa soVMkilalxda. 
\num{6} BwtikavAgi asitxtavxdalilxruva; pAramAthiRkavalalxda yA bwdidhxkavalalxda yA kAlapxnikavalalxda. 
\num{7} Bwtika vasutxgaLige saMbaMdhisida: \eng{the natural world} Bwtika parxpaMca. 
\num{8} nisagaRdalilx beLediruva; sahaja rUpadalilx, sithxtiyalilx iruva; kaqtakavalalxda. 
\num{9} (sasayxgaLa \vi) tAneV tAnAgi huTiTxda; savxyaMjAta; vayxvasAyadiMda beLesirada. 
\num{10} (jamiVnina \vi) beVsAya mADirada; vayxvasAya mADilalxda. 
\num{11} savxBAvasidadhx; aMtagaRta; aMtaBURta. 
\num{12} sahaja; jiVvaMtavAgiruvaMte toVruva. 
\num{13} sahaja; saraLa; naTaneyalalxda; kaqtakavalalxda; kaqtirxmavalalxda: \eng{natural voice} sahaja dhavxni. \eng{a piece of natural acting} sahaja aBinaya. 
\num{14} sahaja; sAvxBAvika; AshacxyaRkaravalalxda; niriVkiSxsabahudAdaMtha: \eng{it is natural for a bird to fly} hakikx hAruvudu sahajaveV, AshacxyaRveVnalalx; hAruvudu hakikxya sahaja guNa. 
\num{15} virUpagoLisada; rUpa mArevADada. 
\num{16} sahaja; parxkaqtisidadhx; huTiTxniMda baruva; sulaBavAgi baruva; tAneV tAnAgi odaguva: \eng{he is a natural orator} avanobabx huTuTx vAgimx. \eng{comes natural to him} adu avanige sahajavAgi barutatxde. 
\num{17} sahaja; sAvxBAvika; savxBAvadiMda aMtiruva yA aMtAguva; hAgirabeVkeMdu huTuTxvAgaleV parxkaqti nidhaRrisidaMte toVruva: \eng{natural enemies} huTuTx hagegaLu. \eng{the natural antithesis} sahaja viroVdha. 
\num{18} keVvala pArxkaqta, deYhika saMbaMdhada; vivAhabAhayx; vivAheVtara saMbaMdhadalilx huTiTxda: \eng{natural son} vivAheVtara saMbaMdhada maga. 
\num{19} kAnUnu bAhayx; hAdarada: \eng{a natural child} jAraja shishu; hAdarada magu. 
\num{20} nisagARdhayxyanada; parxkaqtiyanunx kuritu adhayxyana mADuva.

\bentry
\word{naturalism}
\pron{nAYxcaralisaZmf}
\gl{\nA}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} sahaja kirxye; sAvxBAvika kirxye; sahaja parxvaqtitxgaLiMda parxcoVditavAda kirxye; sahaja parxvaqtitxgaLiMda parxcoVditavAda kirxye, kAyaR. 
\hypertarget{naturalism(2)}{} 
\num{2} pArxkaqtika dhamaR; neYsagiRka dhamaR; sahaja dhamaR; keVvala parxkaqtiyanunx, nisagaRvanunx Adharisiruva niVti shAsatxrX yA matadhamaR. 
\numi{3} (\tashA) parxkaqti vAda; nisagaR vAda; savxBAva vAda; BwtavAda; 
\banum
\alnum{a} jagatitxna saqSiTxge matutx sithxtige yAvudeV nisagARtiVta yA AdhAyxtimxka kAraNa matutx shakitx beVkAgilalx, adu savxtaMtarx savxyaMBu savxyaMpUNaR matutx savxyaM niyaMtarxka, adu EkameVvAdivxtiVya satayx, mAnava adara oMdu aMga -- eMba sidAdhxMta; jagatatxnunx kuritaMte yAvudeV atimAnuSa yA AdhAyxtimxka parigaNaneyanunx nirAkarisuva daqSiTx, vAda; keVvala neYsagiRka kAraNagaLu matutx niyamagaLu jagatitxnalilx elalxvanUnx vivarisabalalxveMba vAda. 
\alnum{b} elalx neYtika niNaRyagaLU vasutxniSaThx vaNaRnegaLu matutx avanunx pArxyoVgikavAgi pariVkiSxsabahudu eMba vAda. 
\alnum{c} (\deVva) matadhamaRda elalx tatatxvXgaLU nisagaRda kirxyegaLa adhayxyanadiMdaleV anugatavAgutatxve, avakekx deVva parxkAshana beVkAgilalx eMba vAda. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{4} (sAhitayx, kale) yathAthaR citarxNa; yathAthaRvAda; vAsatxvikate; vAsatxvika badukanunx AdashiRVkarisade, adu iruvaMteyeV pUNaR vivaragaLoMdige vasutxniSaThxvAgi, neYtika niNaRyagaLa soVMkilalxde, yathAvatAtxgi citirxsuva, vaNiRsuva vidhAna yA adanunx kurita sidAdhxMta.

\bentry
\word{nature}

\gl{\nA}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} (asitxtavxkekx AvashayxkavAda) vasutxvina sahaja -- guNa, savxrUpa, lakaSxNa, dhamaR. 
\num{2} (aneVka veVLe \eng{Nature)}(manuSayxna, pArxNiya) parxkaqti; savxBAva: \eng{it is not in her nature to act like that} A riVti naDeyuvudu avaLa savxBAvavalalx. 
\num{3} manuSayx jAtiya savxBAva, lakaSxNa matutx BAvanegaLu. 
\num{4} manuSayx savxBAvada vishiSaTx aMsha: \eng{the rational nature} veYcArika savxBAva. \eng{animal nature} pashu (pArxyavAda) savxBAva. \eng{moral nature} neYtika savxBAva. 
\num{5} vishiSaTx savxBAvavuLaLx vayxkitx: \eng{sanguine natures do not feel this}... AshAvAdi savxBAvadavarige, AshAvAdigaLige idara arivu iruvudilalx. 
\num{6} tera; bage; riVti; vagaR: \eng{things of this nature of a request} idu koVrikeya riVtiyadu. 
\num{7} (manuSayxna shiVlavanunx, kirxyeyanunx nidhaRrisuva AMtarika) parxvaqtitxgaLu; perxVraNegaLu.

\num{11} sasayx, pArxNi, BUdaqshayx, \mo\ nisagaRda aMshagaLu: \eng{nature gives him comfort} nisagaR avanige nemamxdi koDutatxde.

\bentry

\gl{\nA}
\bmng

\enum
\emng

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}
{\eng{say nay} `Agadu', `ilalx' inunxvudu; `uhuM' eMdu heVLuvudu: \eng{cannot say him nay} avanige Agadu enanxlAgadu.}\eentry

\num{2} (\pArxparx) bahumaTiTxge; inunx savxlapxdaralilx: \eng{he was as near as could be to being knocked down by a bus} savxlapxdaralilx basusx avana meVle haridu hoVguvudaralilxtutx. 
\num{3} hatitxra hatitxra: \eng{as near as one can guess, there were forty people} hatitxra hatitxra alilx nalavatutx janaridadxru. 
\num{4} (\pArxparx) bahaLa lekAkxcAravAgi; jipuNatanadiMda: \eng{he lives very near} avanu bahaLa jipuNatanadiMda jiVvana naDesutAtxne. 
\enum
\emng

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}
\bmng

\bnum

\num{2} (oMdu kelasa mADalu, obabxnanunx) nibaRMdhisu; balAtakxrisu: \eng{each boy is necessitated to act for himself} parxtiyobabx huDuganU tanagAgi tAnu kelasa mADaleV beVkAgide. 
\enum
\emng

\num{4} baDatana; nigaRti; Avashayxka vasutxgaLa aBAva. 
\num{5} Avashayxkate; Avashayxka vasutx; beVkAdudu: \eng{my needs are few} nananx agatayxgaLu bahaLa savxlapxveV. 
\enum
\emng

\num{3} (kataRvayx \mo vugaLa \vi) avajacnxte; udAsiVnate; asaDeDx; upeVkeSx: \eng{he lost his job because of neglect of duty} tananx kataRvayxda bagegx upeVkeSx toVrisidadxriMda avanu kelasa kaLedukoMDa. 
\enum
\emng

\alnum{b} naroVderxVka; tiVkaSxNXvAda, aneVka veVLe unAmxda keraLisuva naragaLa sithxti.

\bmng

\num{3} (mucucxva, aDakavAgisuva, rakaSxNeya, tuMbi hiDidukoMDu hoVguva, \mo\ upayoVgagaLuLaLx) bale. 
\num{4} (PuTfbAlf \mo\ ATagaLalilx goVlf parxdeVshavanunx mucacxlu, Tenisf \mo\ ATagaLalilx ATada parxdeVshavanunx viBAgisalu hAkuva) bale.

\bentry
\word{news}
\pron{nUyxsfZ}
\gl{\nA}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} (\sA\ \Eva vAgi \parx) sudidx; vAteR; samAcAra; (hosa) vataRmAna; vaqtAtxMta; hosa viSaya; hosa GaTane: \eng{have you heard this news}I sudidx keVLididxVyeVnu? 
\num{2} sudidx parxsAra mAdhayxma. 
\num{3} (kulxpatx, hosa) sudidx samAcAragaLa bAnuli parxsAra. 
\num{4} \eng{News}(vaqtatxpatirxkegaLa hesarina BAgavAgi baruva) samAcAra patirxke, \udA\ \eng{Evening News}. 
\enum
\emng

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}
\bmng
\bnum
\numi{1} \eng{bad news} 
\banum
\alnum{a} keTaTx sudidx; ashuBa vAteR. 
\alnum{b} (\AmA) ahitakara vayxkitx yA vasutx. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{2} \eng{be news} (Iga tAneV keVLida) hosa viSaya: \eng{that is news to me} A sudidx nAnu I tanaka keVLiyeV iralilalx. 
\num{3} \eng{good news} shuBavAteR; oLeLxya sudidx. 
\hyperdef{N}{news pagu(4)}{} 
\num{4} \eng{no news is good news} sudidxyilalxdiruvudeV oMdu oLeLx sudidx; sudidxyilalxdiruvudu oLeLxya sithxtiyanunx sUcisutatxde. 
\num{5} \eng{that is no news} adu elalxrigU gotitxruva samAcAra; adeVnU hosa sudidxyalalx. 
\num{6} \eng{be in the news} (sudidxyanunxMTumADuvaSuTx) parxsidadhxvAgu: \eng{she was in the news last year} hoVda vaSaR avaLadedxV sudidx. 
\enum
\emng

\bentry

\pron{nekfsfTx}
\gl{\nA}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} pakakxda, samiVpada -- vayxkitx, vasutx, \mo vu.

\num{3} muMdina kAgada, saMcike, \mo vu: \eng{will tell you in my next} nananx muMdina kAgadadalilx heVLutetxVne. 
\num{4} muMdina vAra \mo vu: \eng{the Friday after next} muMdina shukarxvArada anaMtarada shukarxvAra.

\emng

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}
\bmng
\hyperdef{N}{next(4) pagu(1)}{} 
\bnum
\num{1} \eng{next of kin}(badukiruvavaralilx) hatitxrada naMTaru; samiVpa baMdhugaLu. 
\numi{2} \eng{next please} 
\banum
\alnum{a} idu sAku, muMdina parxshenx keVLi. 
\alnum{b} nimamxdu Ayitu, muMdinavanu barali. 
\eanum
\numie

\emng

\bentry
\word{night}
\pron{neYTf}
\gl{\nA}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} iruLu; rAtirx; nishe; sUyARsatxdiMda sUyoRVdayadavaregina kAla. 
\num{2} iruLa katatxle: \eng{went forth into the night} katatxloLakekx hoVda. 
\num{3} (\alaMshA) aMdhakAra sithxti; tamasusx; rAtirxya katatxlinaMtha sithxti. 
\num{4} mucacxMje; mabubx; saMdhAyxkAla; muMgatatxle: \eng{shall not reach home before night} mucacxMjeya oLage (katatxlu kaviyuva munanx) mane talupalAre. 
\num{5} rAtirxya -- have, anuBavagaLu yA kelasa kAyaRgaLu. 
\num{6} (nATaka \mo) parxdashaRnagaLu naDeyuva saMje: \eng{first night} nATakada modalaneya (rAtirx) parxdashaRna. 
\enum
\emng

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}
\bmng
\hypertarget{night pagu1}{} 
\bnum
\num{1} \eng{all night} iruLelalx; rAtirxyiDiV. 
\num{2} \eng{all night long} = \hyperlink{night pagu1}{?pagu?\((1)\)}. 
\num{3} \eng{at night} saMjeyalilx; katatxlAda meVle; rAtirxyalilx; saMje \eng{6}riMda madhayxrAtirxyavaregina kAladalilx: \eng{ten o'clock at night}rAtirx hatutx gaMTe. 
\num{4} \eng{black} (\engit{or} \eng{dark) as night} rAtirxyaMtha kapupx; iruLugapupx; iruLinaMtha katatxlu. 
\num{5} \eng{by night} rAtirxyalilx; iruLa mareyalilx. 
\num{6} \eng{have a bad night} rAtirx niderxyilalxde bAdhepaDu. 
\num{7} \eng{have a good night} rAtirx suKa niderx mADu. 
\num{8} \eng{last night} hiMdina, kaLeduhoVda, atayxMta Icina -- rAtirx. 
\num{9} \eng{make a night of it} rAtirxyelAlx utasxva samAraMBadalilx kaLe. 
\num{10} \eng{night and day} hagaliruLU; eDebiDade; yAvAgalU; sadA. 
\num{11} \eng{spend the night with} (\sA\ leYMgika saMbaMdhavanunx sUcisuva athaRdalilx) (\kanmu) rAtirx malagalu avakAsha paDe. 
\num{12} \eng{stay the night} rAtirx taMgu; (maneyiMdAce) beLagAguvavarege uLiduko. 
\num{13} \eng{turn night into day} dinada hAge rAtirx iDiV (agatayxvAda ujavxla diVpagaLa beLakinalilx) kelasa mADu. 
\num{14} \eng{work nights} rAtirxya saradiyalilxru. 
\enum
\emng

\num{5} \eng{nine times out of ten} (\birx) sAmAnayxvAgi; bahuteVka; mukAkxlu mUru viVse pAlu. 
\num{6} \eng{nine to five} oMbatatxriMda aidaravarege: sAmAnayxvAgi kaceVriya kelasada veVLe. 
\num{7} \eng{possession is nine points of the law} oMdu vasutxvina sAvxdhiVnAnuBavavidadxre adara meVle hatatxralilx oMbatutx pAlu nAyxyAnukUlavAda hakukx idadxMteyeV.

\enum

\pron{nAmineVTivf}
\gl{\gu}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} nAmakaraNada; nAmakaraNa mADuva; nAmakaraNakekx saMbaMdhisida: \eng{the nominative and elective principles} nAmakaraNa mADuva hAgU Ayekx mADuva sUtarxgaLu. 
\num{2} nAmakaraNadiMda neVmisida. 
\enum
\emng
\eentry

\bentry

\bentry
\word{non-}
\pron{nAnf-}
\gl{\pUparx}
\bmng
niSeVdhAthaRka \pUparx, \kanmu\ 
\bnum
\num{1} mADada, ilalxda yA saMbaMdhapaDada: \eng{non-attendance} hAjarAgadiruvike; geYru hAjari. \eng{non-payment} pAvati mADadiruvudu. 
\num{2} vivarisida vagaRkekx, bagege -- seVrada; \eng{non-alcoholic} AlakxhAlf vagaRkekx seVrada. \eng{non-member} sadasayxra vagaRkekx seVrada; sadasayxnalalxda. 
\num{3} \gu vAgi baLasuva padagaLanunx racisuvalilx: \eng{non-party} pakaSxkekx seVrirada; pakASxtiVtavAda. 
\num{4} ilalxda; aBAvada: \eng{non-access} parxveVsha (mAgaR) ilalxda. 
\num{5} (\kirxvi gaLoDane) heVLiruva riVtiyalilx ilalxda: \eng{non-aggressively} AkarxmaNakAriyAgilalxde. 
\num{6} kirxyApadagaLiMda Agada, mADada, udedxVshakakxlalxda eMba athaRda \gu gaLanunx racisuvalilx: \eng{non-skid} jArada. 
\num{7} \eng{in-} yA \eng{un-} \pUparx gaLiMda racitavAda niSeVdhAthaRka shabadxgaLu vishiSATxthaRvoMdanonxV virudAdhxthaRvoMdanonxV koDuva yA visheVSavalalxda sAmAnayx niSeVdhAthaRvanunx koDuva padagaLanunx racisuvalilx: \eng{non-effective} pariNAmakAriyalalxda. \eng{non-human} mAnavanalalxda (Adare amAnaviVyavAgirada). 
\enum
\emng
\eentry

\bentry

\gl{\sanA}
\bmng
oMdU alalx; obabxnU alalx; yAvudU alalx: \eng{none of them came} avaralilx obabxnU baralilalx. \eng{none of this concerns me} idaralilx yAvudU nanage (savxlapxvU) saMbaMdhisilalx. \eng{none but fools have ever believed it} mUKaRralalxde (mUKaRranunx biTuTx) beVre yArU idanunx eMdU naMbilalx. 
\emng

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}
\bmng
\eng{none other} beVre yArU alalx, ilalx. 
\emng

\num{2} oMdu nidiRSaTx jAtige, vagaRkekx seVrisalAgada: \eng{if a linguist is wanted, I am none} BASA vijAcnxni beVkAgidadxre, nAnaMtU alalx.

\bentry
\word[Norse(1)]{Norse}
\pron{nAsfR}
\gl{\nA}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} nAveR deVshada BASe. 
\num{2} sAkx YxMDineVviyanf BASegaLa vagaR. 
\numi{3} \eng{(the Norse)}(\bava vAgi \parx) 
\banum
\alnum{a} nAveR deVshadavaru. 
\alnum{b} \eng{$8-10$}ne shatamAnagaLalilxdadx, vAyavayx yUroVpina BAgagaLalilx nelasidadx kaDalugaLaLxru, veYkiMgfgaLu. 
\eanum
\numie
\enum
\emng

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}
\bmng
\eng{Old Norse} 
\banum
\alnum{a} sAkx yxMDineVviyada BASegaLa mUlavAda jamAYxRnikf BASe. 
\alnum{b} \eng{$14$}neya shatamAnadavaregina nAveR matutx adara vasAhatugaLa BASe. 
\eanum
\emng
\eentry

\bmng

\num{2} \eng{north by east} utatxrakUkx utatxreVshAnayxkUkx naDuvaNa. 
\num{3} \eng{north by west} utatxrakUkx utatxra vAyuvayxkUkx naDuvaNa. 
\num{4} \eng{the North West} vAyavayx parxdeVsha (\kanmu\ kenaDa). 
\num{5} \eng{to the north of}... diMda utatxrakekx. 
\enum
\emng
\eentry

\bentry
\word[north(2)]{north}
\pron{nAtfR}
\gl{\nA}
\bmng
\bnum
\numi{1} 
\banum
\alnum{a} baDaga; utatxra (dikukx). 
\alnum{b} dikUsxciyalilx idakekx sariyAgiruva biMdu. 
\alnum{c} I biMduviruva dikukx. 
\eanum
\numie
\numi{2} (\sA \eng{the North}) 
\banum
\alnum{a} parxpaMcada yA deVshada yA nagarada utatxra dikikxnalilxruva parxdeVsha, utatxraBAga. 
\alnum{b} AkfRTikf parxdeVsha; BUmiya utatxradhurxvada parxdeVsha, utatxra valaya. 
\alnum{c} keYgArikA rASaTxrXgaLu; keYgArikoVdayxmagaLalilx aBivaqdidhx sAdhisida rASaTxrXgaLu. 
\alnum{d} (\kanmu) iMgelxMDina utatxraBAga yA amerikasaMsAthxnagaLa utatxrarAjayxgaLu. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{3} \eng{(North)}(birxDfjx isipxVTATa) ``utatxra" eMdu hesarisiruva kaDe kuLitu ADuva ATagAra. 
\enum
\emng

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}
\bmng
\eng{North Briton} (\pArxparx) sAkxTelxMDf (parxdeVsha). 
\emng
\eentry

\bentry
\word[nose(1)]{nose}
\pron{noVsf}
\gl{\nA}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} mUgu; nAsika; GArxNeVMdirxya. 
\num{2} GArxNashakitx; vAsane hiDiyuva shakitx. 
\num{3} (oNahululx, TiV, madayx, hogesopupx, \mo vugaLa) vAsane; kaMpu; gaMdha. 
\num{4} (nALa, koLave, tidi, bakapAterx, \mo vugaLa) mUti; tereda tudi. 
\num{5} haDagina, doVNiya -- mUti, cAcuBAga. 
\num{6} = \hyperlink{nosing}{nosing}. 
\num{7} (moVTArf kAru, vimAna, \mo vugaLa) muMBAga; mUti. 
\num{8} (\ashi) rahasayx varadigAra; aparAdhigaLanunx patetx mADi, poliVsarige avara bagegx mAhiti koDuvavanu. 
\enum
\emng

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} \eng{as plain as the nose on your face} sapxSaTxvAgide; sapxSaTxvAgi kANisuvaMtide. 
\num{2} \eng{by a nose} atayxlapx aMtaradiMda; savxlapxdaralilx; \eng{won the race by a nose} atayxlapx aMtaradiMda paMdayxvanunx gedadx. 
\numi{3} \eng{count noses} 
\banum
\alnum{a} hAjariruvavaranunx, beMbala koDuvavaranunx, anumoVdisuvavaranunx lekakx mADu; mUgeNisu. 
\alnum{b} (oMdu viSayavanunx) keVvala saMKAyxbaladiMda nidhaRrisu. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{4} \eng{ get up a (person's) nose} (\ashi) (obabxnanunx) kADu; piVDisu; reVgisu. 
\numi{5} \eng{has a good nose} curuku mUgide: 
\banum
\alnum{a} (nAyi \mo vugaLa \vi) vAsane hiDiyuva oLeLx shakitx ide. 
\alnum{b} (\rUpa) (gupatx poliVsaru \mo vara \vi) (aparAdha \mo vugaLa) suLivu hiDiyuva, patetx hacucxva -- kwshala, oLeLxya shakitx ide. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{6} \eng{hold one's nose} dunARta tapipxsikoLaLxlu mUgu mucicxko, hoLeLxgaLanunx beraLugaLiMda otitxhiDiduko. 
\num{7} \eng{keep one's nose clean} (\ashi) sariyAgi naDeduko; toMdarege sikikxbiVLada hAgiru. 
\num{8} \eng{keep one's nose to the grindstone} kaSaTxpaTuTx, vishArxMtiyilalxde, niraMtaravAgi duDi, kelasa mADu. 
\num{9} \hyperref{kandict_l.pdf}{L}{look(1) nuga(8)}{$^1$look} \eng{down one's nose at}. 
\num{10} \eng{nose of wax} meVNadaMthavanu yA meVNadaMtha vasutx; sulaBavAgi tidadxbahudAda -- manuSayx, vasutx. 
\numi{11} \eng{on the nose} 
\banum
\alnum{a} (\ame) (\ashi) sariyAgi; karAruvAkAkxgi. 
\alnum{b} (\AseTxrXV) (\ashi) reVgisuvaMtha; piVDisuvaMtha. 
\hypertarget{nose pagu12}{} 
\eanum
\numie

\numie

\bentry
\word{not}
\pron{nATf}
\gl{\kirxvi}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} (\pArxparx) alalx; ilalx: \eng{I know not} nanage gotitxlalx. \eng{I doubt not} nanage saMshayavilalx. 
\numi{2} ilalx: 
\banum
\alnum{a} (sahAyaka \kirx da jate \eng{n't} seVrisidAga) ilalx: \eng{I can't say} nAnu heVLalAre. \eng{he'll not come} avanu baruvudilalx. (\ashi) \eng{he ain't here} avanililxlalx. 
\alnum{b} (vidhuyxkatx heVLikeyalilx) \eng{did you not tell me} niVnu nanage heVLalilalxveV? 
\eanum
\numie
\num{3} kaqdaMtagaLanunx dhAtavxthaRvAcigaLa hiMde niSeVdhAthaR sUcakavAgi baLasuvAga: \eng{not knowing} tiLiyade. \eng{asked him not to come} barabeVDaveMdu avanige heVLide. 
\num{4} (niSeVdhAthaRka vAkayx, kirxyApada yA padagucaCxgaLige adhAyxhAravAgi baruvAga): \eng{``Are you ill?" ``Not at all"} ninage kAhileyAgideyeV? KaMDita ilalx. \eng{popular or not, it is right} janapirxyavAgirali biDali, adu sariyAda mAtu hwdu. 
\num{5} (payARyavAgi kelavu mAtugaLanunx seVrisutAtx, avugaLalilx kelavanunx niSeVdhisutAtx mAtanADuvAga) `adu adalalx -- Adare adu beVroMdu' enunxva hAge: \eng{he is not my son, but yours} avanu nananx maganalalx, ninanx maga. 
\num{6} (oMdu niSeVdhAthaRsUcaka vAkayxda naMtara baruva savaRnAmavanunx otitx heVLuvAga) \eng{they will not be fooled, not they} avaru moVsa hoVgalAraru -- avare? eMdigU ilalx. 
\num{7} (\eng{`a'} eMba anideRVshaka guNavAciya hiMde baMdAga, `oMdu saha ilalx' eMbathaRdalilx) \eng{not a hair of your head shall be touched} ninanx taleya oMdu kUdalanunx saha muTuTxvudilalx. 
\num{8} (inonxMdu niSeVdha rUpada shabadxda jate, swmAyxthaR sUcaka saMdaBaRdalilx baMdAga) \eng{not a few} alapxsavxlapxvalalx (eMdare `bahaLa' eMbathaRdalilx). \eng{not seldom} aparUpavAgalalx; omomxmemxyalalx (eMdare `aneVka veVLe' eMbathaRdalilx). 
\enum
\emng

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} \eng{as likely as not} eSuTx saMBavavoV aSeTxV asaMBavavU hwdu. 
\num{2} \eng{not at all} (yArAdarU kaqtajacnxte sUcisidAga shiSATxcArakAkxgi utatxra koDutAtx) aMthadeVnU ilalx; hAge niVvu heVLuva agatayxvilalx. 
\num{3} \eng{not a thing} yAvudU ilalx oMdU ilalx. 
\num{4} \eng{not but that} = \hyperlink{notpagu16}{?pagu?\((16)\)}. 
\num{5} \eng{not but}(\pArxparx) = \hyperlink{notpagu16}{?pagu?\((16)\)}. 
\num{6} \eng{no} \hyperref{kandict_h.pdf}{H}{half(3) nuga}{$^3$half}. 
\num{7} \eng{not least} kaDame pArxmuKayxvalalx (eMdare sAkaSuTx parxmuKavAda). 
\num{8} \eng{not} \hyperref{kandict_m.pdf}{M}{much(3) pagu(6)}{$^3$much}. 
\num{9} \eng{not once nor twice} = \hyperlink{notpagu10}{?pagu?\((10)\)}. 
\hypertarget{notpagu10}{} 
\num{10} \eng{not once or twice} oMderaDu salavalalx; aneVka bAri. 
\numi{11} \eng{not quite}: 
\banum
\alnum{a} hecucx kaDame. 
\alnum{b} aSeTxVnU alalx; bahuteVka: \eng{it is not quite proper} adu aSeTxVnU ucitavalalx. 
\hypertarget{notpagu12}{} 
\eanum
\numie
\num{12} \eng{not so well} aSeTxVnU oLeLxyadalalxda (riVtiyalilx). 
\hyperdef{N}{not pagu(13)}{} 
\num{13} \eng{not that} hAgeMdu athaRvalalx, Adare: \eng{if he said so-not that he ever did-he lied} avanu hAge heVLidadxre -- hAge eMdigU heVLiralAra -- adu suLuLx. 
\num{14} \eng{not too well} = \hyperlink{notpagu12}{?pagu?\((12)\)}. 
\num{15} \eng{not} \hyperref{kandict_v.pdf}{V}{very(2) pagu(1)}{$^2$very}. 
\hypertarget{notpagu16}{} 
\numi{16} \eng{not but what}(\pArxparx) 
\banum
\alnum{a} adeVneV irali; AdarU; hAgidadxrU: \eng{ not what I can do it, not but that a stronger man might} nAnu adanunx mADalAre; adeVneV irali nanagiMta shakatxnAdavanu adanunx mADirutitxdadx. 
\alnum{b} aMthadadxlalx; aMthavanalalx: \eng{not such a fool but what he can see it}adanunx kANadiruvaSuTx avanu daDaDxnalalx. 
\eanum
\numie
\enum
\emng
\eentry

\bentry
\word[note(1)]{note}
\pron{noVTf}
\gl{\nA}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} (\sA\ \bava dalilx) (BASaNakAkxgali, leVKanakAkxgali mADikoMDa, nenapiTuTxkoLaLxlu sahAykavAguva) vAsatxvAMshagaLa, viSayagaLa, aBipArxyagaLa -- TipapxNi, muKAyxMshagaLa paTiTx: \eng{make} (\engit{or} \eng{take) notes of} TipapxNi mADiko; muKAyxMshagaLanunx gurutuhAku. \eng{speak without notes} TipapxNi ilalxde mAtanADu. 
\num{2} (anuBavagaLu \mo vugaLa, \sA\ aliKita) kathana. 
\num{3} ciVTi; anwpacArika yA saNaNx patarx. 
\num{4} (pusatxka \mo vugaLalilx garxMthaBAgagaLanunx, viSayagaLanunx vishadapaDisalu seVrisiruva) TipapxNi; vivaraNe; aDiTipapxNi. 
\num{5} (\birx) = \hyperref{kandict_b.pdf}{B}{banknote}{banknote}. 
\num{6} (oMdu gotAtxda avadhiylilx, namUdAda haNa koDuvudAgi baredukoTaTx halavAru riVtiya) keYpatarx (gaLalolxMdu). 
\numi{7} 
\banum
\alnum{a} gamana; lakaSxyX: \eng{worthy of note} gamanAhaRvAda. 
\alnum{b} Ganate; parxsididhx; (parx)KAyxti: \eng{a critic of note} parxsidadhx vimashaRka. \eng{a person of note} parxsidadhx vayxkitx. 
\eanum
\numie
\numi{8} 
\banum
\alnum{a} \saM\ savxracihenx; savxralipi; saMgiVta dhavxniya tiVvarxteya maTaTx matutx avadhiyanunx sUcisuva lipi saMkeVta. 
\alnum{b} (saMgiVtavAdayx, dhavxni, eMjinf, \mo vu mADuva) nidiRSaTx shurxtiy savxra. 
\alnum{c} (piyAnoV \mo\ vAdayxgaLalilx, dhavxni huTiTxsuva) kiVlikeY.

\banum

\num{11} cihenx; gurutu; lakaSxNa; veYshiSaTxyX: \eng{catholicity is one note of the true church} manoVveYshAlayx nijavAda caciRna oMdu lakaSxNa. 
\num{12} (\pArxparx) kaLaMka; doVSa; KaMDaney cihenx: \eng{on which the law has set a note of infamy} kAnUnu adara meVle apaKAyxtiy kaLaMka horiside. 
\num{13} (\pArxparx) udAgxrada, mecicxkey yA parxshAnxthaRka cihenx, gurutu: \eng{a note of interrogation} parxshAnxthaRka cihenx. 
\num{14} (vidhuyxkatxvAda rAjakiVy) niyoVgapatarx.

\bentry
\word[nothing(1)]{nothing}
\pron{natiMgf}
\gl{\nA}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} (guNavAcakada hiMde baMdAga) yAvudeV vasutx alalx, ilalx(dudx): \eng{nothing great is easy} mahatavxvAdadudx yAvudU sulaBavalalx. \eng{nothing has been done} EnanUnx mADalAgilalx; yAvudU Agilalx. \eng{have nothing to do} mADalu (kelasa) EnU ilalx. 
\num{2} (kelamomemx pUrakavAkayxda joteylilx) yAvudU, EnU ilalx: \eng{I see nothing that I want} nanage beVkAda yAvudU nanage kANutitxlalx. \eng{can find nothing useful} upayukatxvAda yAvudU ilalx. 
\numi{3} 
\banum
\alnum{a} kuSxlalxkavAda -- vasutx, saMgati, mAtu yA vayxkitx: \eng{was nothing to me} adu nanage kuSxlalxkavAda viSayavAgitutx. \eng{the little nothings of life} jiVvanada kuSxlalxka viSayagaLu. \eng{he is nothing without his money} avana baLi haNavilalxde hoVgidadxre avanobabx kelasakekx bArada vayxkitx. 
\alnum{b} (visheVSaNavAgi, \AmA) agaNayx; beleyilalxda: \eng{a nothing sort of day} oMdu riVti agaNayxvAda dina. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{4} aBAva; ilalxme; ilalxdiruvike; ilalxdiruvudu; nAsitx. 
\num{5} (aMkagaNita, lekAkxcAradalilx) sonenx -- aMka, mobalagu, itAyxdi: \eng{multiply 6 by nothing, and the result is nothing} Aranunx sonenxyiMda guNisidare sonenx barutatxde. \eng{a third of nothing is nothing} sonenxya mUraneV oMdu BAga sonenxyeV. 
\enum
\emng

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}
\bmng
\bnum
\numi{1} \eng{be nothing}(dhamaRda \vi) 
\banum
\alnum{a} yAva nidiRSaTx paMgaDakUkx seVradiru. 
\alnum{b} nAsitxkanAgiru. 
\alnum{c} ajecnxVyatAvAdiyAgiru. 
\eanum
\numie
\numi{2} \eng{be nothing to} 
\banum
\alnum{a} saMbaMdha beVDadiru; saMbaMdhisiradiru: \eng{it is nothing to do with me} adakUkx nanagU saMbaMdhavilalx. 
\alnum{b} hoVlikeyAgadiru; hoVlike ilalxdiru. 
\eanum
\numie
\numi{3} \eng{be} (\engit{or} \eng{have) nothing to do with} 
\banum
\alnum{a} (vasutx yA vayxkitxya \vi) saMbaMdha ilalxdiru; goDave ilalxdiru; usAbari beVDadiru. 
\alnum{b} (yAvudeV oMdaralilx yA oMdaroDane) saMbaMdha hoMdadiru, seVradiru. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{4} \eng{come to nothing} niSaPxlavAgu; vayxthaRvAgi pariNamisu; EnU parxyoVjanavAgadiru: \eng{hopes that come to nothing} vayxthaRvAgi pariNamisuva BaravasegaLu; niSapxla niriVkeSxgaLu. 
\num{5} \eng{count} (\engit{or} \eng{go) for nothing} gaNanege bAradiru; vayxthaRvAgu. 
\num{6} \eng{feel like nothing on earth}(\AmA) tiVvarxvAda asavxsathxte yA mujugara anuBavisu. 
\numi{7} \eng{for nothing} 
\banum
\alnum{a} pukakxTeyAgi. 
\alnum{b} vayxthaRvAgi; EnU parxyoVjanavilalxde. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{8} \eng{has nothing in him} avanobabx nagaNayx; yaHkashicxtf manuSayx; avanige yAva vayxkitxtavxvU ilalx. 
\hyperdef{N}{nothing(1) pagu(9)}{} 
\numi{9} \eng{have nothing on} 
\banum
\alnum{a} (yAvudoV oMdakikxMta) hecucx anukUla hoMdilalxdiru. 
\alnum{b} (obabxna bagegx) AkeSxVpaNiVyavAda EnanUnx hoMdadiru, gotitxlalxdiru. 
\alnum{c} (vayxMgayx) (yAvudoV oMdakikxMta) tiVrA kiVLAgiru. 
\alnum{d} bari meYyalilxru; betatxleyAgiru. 
\alnum{e} biDuvAgiru; yAvudeV kelasakAyRgaLilalxdiru. 
\eanum
\numie
\numi{10} \eng{is nothing to} 
\banum
\alnum{a} EnU lekakxvilalx; yAvudakUkx ilalx; taqNasamAna: \eng{money is nothing to him} haNa eMdare avanige taqNasamAna. 
\alnum{b} (adara) samAnakekx baralAradu; (adakUkx, idakUkx) hoVlike ilalx. 
\eanum
\numie
\numi{11} \eng{like nothing on earth}(\AmA) (kurUpa \mo vugaLa \vi) atayxMta; vipariVtavAda; ati hecicxna: \eng{look like nothing on earth}(\AmA): 
\banum
\alnum{a} tiVrA avalakaSxNavAgiru; bahaLa kurUpiyAgiru. 
\alnum{b} ati ADaMbaradiMda tuMbiru; kaNiNxge rAcuvaMtiru. 
\eanum
\numie
\numi{12} \eng{make nothing of} 
\banum
\alnum{a} laGuvAgeNisu; alapxveMdu BAvisu. 
\alnum{b} hiMjariyade -- mADu, naDesu. 
\alnum{c} EnU mADalu toVcadiru, athaRvAgadiru. 
\alnum{d} upayoVgisalu, baLasalu sAdhayxvilalxvAgu. 
\alnum{e} vayxvaharisalu sAdhayxvilalxvAgu. 
\eanum
\numie
\numi{13} \eng{mean nothing to} 
\banum
\alnum{a} athaRvilalxvAgu. 
\alnum{b} mecacxdaMtAgu. 
\alnum{c} AshisadaMtAgu. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{14} \eng{neck or nothing} AdadAdxgaleMdu; savaRsavxvanUnx paNavAgi oDiDx. 
\num{15} \eng{no nothing}(\AmA) (ilalxda padAthaRgaLa paTiTxyalilx heVLuva koneya mAtu) yAvudU ilalx; oMdU ilalx: \eng{no bread, no butter, no cheese, no nothing}berxDf ilalx, beNeNx ilalx, ciVsfZ ilalx, yAvudU ilalx. 
\num{16} \eng{nothing but} = \hyperlink{nothingpagu18}{?pagu?\((18)\)}. 
\numi{17} \eng{nothing doing} 
\banum
\alnum{a} (\AmA) muKayxvAdadudx EnU sAdhayxvAgadu; gamanAhaRvAdudeVnU Agutitxlalx: \eng{there was nothing doing in town} Urinalilx gamanAhaRvAdudeVnU naDeyutitxlalx. 
\alnum{b} KaMDita ilalx; eMdeMdigU sAdhayxvilalx. 
\hypertarget{nothingpagu18}{} 
\eanum
\numie
\num{18} \eng{nothing else but} (\engit{or} \eng{than)} sumamxne; keVvala; baride; nisasxMdeVhavAgi; nisasxMshayavAgi: \eng{did nothing but grumble} goNaguvudanunx biTuTx EnanUnx mADalilalx; sumamxne (goNagida). 
\num{19} \eng{nothing for it but to} vidhiyilalx; upAyavilalx; adanunx biTuTx beVre mAgaRvilalx. 
\num{20} \eng{nothing if not} muKayxvAgi; mUlataH: \eng{it is nothing if not critical} tapupx kaMDuhiDiyuvudu biTuTx beVreVnU alalx; tapupx kaMDu hiDiyuvudoMdeV muKayx lakaSxNa. 
\numi{21} \eng{nothing less than} 
\banum
\alnum{a} kaDime Enalalx: \eng{expected nothing less than a riot} kaDeV pakaSx doMbi AgutatxdeMdeV niriVkiSxsida; doMbiyAdarU AgiyeV tiVrutatxdeMdu niriVkiSxsida. 
\alnum{b} (\viparx) idakekx tiVrA virudadhxvAda. 
\alnum{c} (\viparx) eMdeMdigU ilalx; savxlapxvU ilalx. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{22} \eng{nothing like leather} tananx saraku elalx kelasakUkx odagutatxde (eMba sAvxBimAnada aBipArxya). 
\num{23} \eng{nothing venture nothing have}(gelalxbeVkAdare mununxgagxbeVku eMbathaRdalilx) dheYyaRvU ilalx, lABavU ilalx. 
\num{24} \hyperref{kandict_s.pdf}{S}{stop(1) pagu(4)}{$^1$stop} \eng{at nothing.} 
\numi{25} \eng{there is nothing in it} 
\banum
\alnum{a} adu nijavalalx. 
\alnum{b} adeVnU muKayxvalalx. 
\alnum{c} adaralilx EnU toDakilalx. 
\alnum{d} (ibabxra peYki) yArigU adaralilx hecicxna parxyoVjana yA anukUla ilalx. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{26} \eng{there is nothing to it} adu nijavalalx; adeVnU muKayxvalalx; adu tiVrA saraLa, neVra. 
\num{27} \eng{think nothing of it}(kaSxme keVLabeVDa yA kaqtajacnxte toVrisabeVkeMba BAvaneyiTuTxkoLaLxbeVDa eMdu sUcisalu baLasuva mAtAgi) adanunx yoVcisabeVDa; hAge ciMtisabeVDa. 
\num{28} \eng{to nothing} karxmeVNa saMpUNaRvAgi -- horaTuhoVgi, kANadAgi, adaqshayxvAgi. 
\num{29} \eng{to say nothing (of)}(aSuTx muKayxvalalxda aMshavanunx heVLuvAga yA muKayx aMshavanunx AlaMkArikavAgi heVLuvAga) (adanunx) heVLabeVkAdudilalx. 
\numi{30} \eng{with nothing on} 
\banum
\alnum{a} betatxleyAgi; barimeYyalilx. 
\alnum{b} sAkaSuTx (meYmucucxvaSuTx) baTeTx hAkikoLaLxde. 
\eanum
\numie
\enum
\emng

\bentry

\pron{nw}
\gl{\kirxvi}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} Iga; sadayxdalilx; I hotitxnalilx; I hotitxge. 
\num{2} I -- kaSxNa, kUDaleV; tatfkaSxNa: \eng{I must go home now} I kaSxNa nAnu manege hoVgabeVku. 
\num{3} ukatx kAladalilx; heVLida -- hotitxnalilx, samayadalilx. 
\num{4} I yA A -- hotitxge, kAlakekx! \eng{it was now clear} A hotitxge adu sapxSaTxvAgitutx. 
\num{5} Iga; parxkaqta saMdaBaRdalilx: \eng{I cannot now agree} parxkaqta saMdaBaRdalilx nAnu opapxlu sAdhayxvilalx. 
\num{6} I muMdina saninxveVshadalilx, parisithxtiyalilx: \eng{I cannot now ever believe you again} inunx eMdigU nAnu ninanxnunx naMbalAre. 
\num{7} I hiMde; savxlapx hiMde; Iga tAne: \eng{just now} Iga tAne; savxlapx hotitxna hiMde. 
\num{8} (\kanmu\ kathanadalilx yA saMBASaNeyalilx) Aga; taruvAya; AmeVle; naMtara; anaMtara: \eng{Caeser now marched east} Aga siVsaZrf pUvaR dikikxna kaDe muMduvarida. \eng{now let us consider the second point} AmeVle eraDaneV viSayavanunx parishiVlisoVNa. 
\num{9} (kAlavanunx sUcisade AkeSxVpaNe, beVDike, bedarike, vivaraNe, samajAyiSi, \mo\ saMdaBaRgaLalilx takakxMte dhavxnikoTuTx \parx) ililx keVLi; nAnu -- beVDuteVtxne, otAtxyisutetxVne, ecacxrike koDutitxdedxVne; AdarU idanunx tiLidirabeVku; idanunx opipxkoLaLxbeVku; KaMDitavAgi (eMba athaRgaLalilx \parx): \eng{now what do you mean by it?} hAgeMdare, Enu aMta niVnu heVLoVdu? \eng{now then don`t cry} hoVgali aLabeVDa, sumamxniru. \eng{now, now behave yourself}! noVDu, noVDu, Iga sariyAgi naDeduko! 
\num{10} inunx -- meVle, muMde: \eng{well what do you want now?} sari, inunx muMde ninageVnAgabeVku?

\bentry
\word[number(1)]{number}
\pron{naMbarf}
\gl{\nA}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} aMki; saMKeyx: \eng{six is an even number} Aru eMbudu samasaMKeyx. 
\numi{2} aMki; saMKeyx: 
\banum
\alnum{a} aMkiyanunx sUcisuva shabadx, saMkeVta yA citarx. 
\alnum{b} gurutu, parAmashaRne, \mo vugaLigAgi, oMdu gotAtxda motatxda sherxVNiyalilx yAvudAdarU oMdanunx nideRVshisuvAga adakekx [\udA\ vAhanagaLu, dUravANi, \mo vakekx] koDuva saMKeyx, aMki: \eng{registration number} noVMdaNi saMKeyx. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{3} (janara, vasutxgaLa oTuTx motatx sUcisuva) aMki; saMKeyx: \eng{what number of people are you expecting?} niVnu oTuTx eSuTx saMKeyxya janaranunx niriVkiSxsutitxdidxVye? \eng{the number of accidents has decreased} apaGAtagaLa saMKeyx kaDameyAgide. \eng{twenty in number} (saMKeyxyalilx) ipapxtitxve. 
\num{4} (\bava dalilx) gaNita; aMkagaNita: \eng{not good at numbers} gaNitadalilx kushalanalalx. 
\num{5} (\Eva\ yA \bava dalilx) parxmANa; motatx: \eng{a large number of people} BAri motatxda janaru. \eng{only in small numbers} kaDame parxmANadalilx mAtarx. 
\num{6} aMki; saMKeyx; oMdu sherxVNiyalilx iMtiSaTxneyadu eMdu sUcisuva cihenx (\kanmu\ vaqtatx patirxkeya iMtha saMcike, giVtanATakadalilx yA saMgiVta kaceVriyalilx iMtiSaTxneya hADu, \mo vu). 
\num{7} jate; jote; guMpu; vagaR: \eng{he is of our number} avanu namamx guMpinavanu. \eng{among our number} namamx guMpinalilx. 
\num{8} (\vAyx) vacana: \eng{Sanskrit has three numbers} saMsakxqqta BASeyalilx mUru vacanagaLive. 
\num{9} (\AmA) (saligeyiMda yA pirxVtiyiMda vayxkitxyanunx yA vasutxvanunx kareyuvAga) naMbaru; isamu: \eng{an attractive little number} AkaSaRkavAda puTaTx vayxkitx, vasutx. 
\num{10} \eng{(Numbers)}(\beY) saMKAyxkAMDa; haLeya oDaMbaDikeyalilx janagaNatiyiruva nAlakxneya adhAyxya. 
\num{11} oMdu gotAtxda saMKeyxyavaregiruvudaralilx nidiRSaTxvAgi yAvudAdarU oMdu vasutx, vayxkitx, \mo vu: \eng{number 22 wants his boots} ipapxtetxraDaneya isamu, vayxkitx bUTugaLu beVkenunxtAtxne. 
\num{12} (\AmA) vayxkitx, uDupu, kelasa, \mo vu. 
\num{13} (\bava dalilx) saMKAyxbala; saMKeyxya hecacxLa: \eng{they won by force of numbers} avaru keVvala saMKAyxbaladiMda gedadxru. 
\num{14} eNike. 
\num{15} (\pArxparx) tALa; laya. 
\numi{16} (\bava dalilx) 
\banum
\alnum{a} (\saM) savxrataMDa. 
\alnum{b} (\CaM) gaNagaLu. 
\alnum{c} (padayxda) sAlugaLu; caraNagaLu; paMkitxgaLu. 
\alnum{d} padayxgaLu; kAvayx: \eng{I lisped in numbers for the numbers came} nAnu todalu mAtanADutitxruvaMteyeV kAvayx raciside; yAkeMdare kAvayx nananxlilx tAneV tAnAgi suPxrisitu. 
\eanum
\numie
\enum
\emng

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}
\bmng
\bnum
\numi{1} \eng{a number of} 
\banum
\alnum{a} kelavu. 
\alnum{b} halavAru; aneVka (\bava da kirxyApadadoDane baLake Iga sAmAnayx): \eng{a number of problems remain} halavAru samaseyxgaLu hAgeyeV uLidive. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{2} \eng{by numbers} saMKAyxnusAra; saMKeyxgaLiMda sUcitavAda saraLa nideRVshagaLanunx anusarisi. 
\num{3} \eng{have a person's number}(\ashi) obabxna nijavAda savxBAva, udedxVsha, \mo vanunx tiLiduko, athaRmADiko. 
\num{4} \eng{have a person's number on it}(bAMbf guMDu, \mo vugaLa \vi) nidiRSaTx vayxkitxyanunx hoDeyuvaMte niyatavAgiru. 
\num{5} \eng{in number} eNikeyalilx; eNisidalilx; saMKeyxyalilx: \eng{one people exceeds another in number} oMdu janAMga inonxMdanunx saMKeyxyalilx miVrisutatxde. 
\num{6} \eng{in numbers}(kathe \mo\ parxkaTaNegaLa \vi) anukarxmavAgi baruva saMcikegaLalilx; saMKAyxnukarxmada BAgagaLalilx. 
\num{7} \eng{in small number} kaDime saMKeyxyalilx; viraLa parxmANadalilx. 
\num{8} \eng{make one's number with}(\ashi) (obabxna jote) saMpakaR hoMdu; obabxnanunx BeVTiyAgu, kANu, saMpakiRsu. 
\num{9} \eng{numbers game} (\hiV) keVvala aMkagaNitada (lekAkxcAra)vanonxLagoMDa kelasa. 
\num{10} \eng{Number Ten} hatutx; DwniMgf siTxrXVTf; iMgelxMDina parxdhAniya adhikaqta laMDanf nivAsa. 
\num{11} \eng{number two} eraDaneya sAthxnadalilxruva; divxtiVya sAthxnada. 
\num{12} \eng{one's number is up}(\AmA) avanu sAyutAtxne; avana kathe mugiyutatxde. 
\num{13} \eng{out of number} = \hyperlink{numberpagu16}{?pagu?\((16)\)}. 
\num{14} \eng{round numbers} (cilalxre saMKeyx biTuTx baruva) pUNARMkagaLu; pUNaR saMKeyxgaLu (\udA\ \eng{10, 20, 100,} \mo vu). 
\num{15} \eng{to the number of}(yAvudoV) aMkiyavarege; saMKeyxyavarege: \eng{to the number of 80} eMbatatxravarege. 
\hypertarget{numberpagu16}{} 
\num{16} \eng{without number} asaMKAyxta; agaNita; lekakxvilalxdaSuTx. 
\enum
\emng
\eentry

\bentry

\bmng

\eanum
\numie
\num{2} gaTiTx biVjaviruva biVjakoVsha.

\num{4} (\ashi) tale; talekAyi ; taleburuDe. 
\numi{5} (\ashi) 
\banum
\alnum{a} hucacx; tikakxla(manuSayx). 
\alnum{b} Bakatx; kaTATx aBimAni: perxVmi: \eng{an exercise nut} vAyxyAmada Bakatx, kaTATxBimAni. 
\eanum
\numie

\alnum{b} (piTiVlu \mo\ taMtivAdayxgaLalilxna) kudure; taMtigaLu hAyuvaMte vAdayxda kaMThada tudiyalilx neleyAgi nililxsiruva kudure. 
\eanum
\numie

\num{9} (\pArxparx) (\ashi) SoVkiVlAla; sogasugAra puTaTxsAmi.

\pron{niMphalepisx}
\gl{\nA}
\bmng
BAvoVnAmxda; dulaRBa vasutxvina moVhadiMdAda AveVsha, unAmxda. 
\emng
\eentry

\bentry
\word{nympholept}
\pron{niMphalepfTx}
\gl{\nA}
\bmng
BAvoVnamxtatx; (\kanmu\ oMdu asAdhayx AdashaRkAkxgi) hucucx utAsxhavuLaLxvanu. 
\emng
\eentry

\bentry
\word{nympholeptic}
\pron{niMphalepiTxkf}
\gl{\gu}
\bmng
BAvoVnAmxdada; hucucx, utAsxhadiMda keraLuva. 
\emng
\eentry

\bentry
\word{nymphomania}
\pron{niMphameVnia}
\gl{\nA}
\bmng
(sitxrXVyara) kAmoVnAmxda; atiyAda kAmApeVkeSx. 
\emng
\eentry

\bentry
\word[nymphomaniac(1)]{nymphomaniac}
\pron{niMphameVniAYxkf}
\gl{\nA}
\bmng
kAvoVnamxtetx; atiyAda kAmApeVkeSxyuLaLx heMgasu. 
\emng
\eentry

\bentry
\word[nymphomaniac(2)]{nymphomaniac}
\pron{niMphameVniAYxkf}
\gl{\gu}
\bmng
(heMgasina \vi) kAmoVnAmxdakekx saMbaMdhisida. 
\emng
\eentry

\bentry
\word{nystagmic}
\pron{nisATx Yxgimxkf}
\gl{\gu}
\bmng
kaNaNxdiru roVgada yA adakekx saMbaMdhisida; akiSxdoVlanada yA adakekx saMbaMdhisida. 
\emng
\eentry

\bentry
\word{nystagmus}
\pron{nisATx Yxgamxsf}
\gl{\nA}
\bmng
kaNaNxdiru roVga; akiSxdoVlana; gaNi kelasagArarige sAmAnayxvAgi baruva, kaNuNxguDeDx eDebiDade alugutitxruva, oMdu bageya roVga. 
\emng
\eentry
